---- systemctl cat scalp-exec.service ----
# /etc/systemd/system/scalp-exec.service
[Unit]
Description=SCALP Exec Engine (FSM SAFE / IDEMPOTENT)
After=network.target
Wants=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
Group=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/scalp/project
ExecStart=/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/exec.py
Restart=always
RestartSec=2
KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10

# Sécurité basique
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

# /etc/systemd/system/scalp-market.service
[Unit]
Description=SCALP - MARKET Collector (ticks + snapshot + volatility)
After=network.target
Requires=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/scalp/project
ExecStart=/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/market_collector.py
Restart=always
RestartSec=5
KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10

# Sécurité minimale (cohérent avec les autres services)
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

After=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/scalp/project

ExecStart=/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/mfe_mae.py

Restart=always
RestartSec=2

# logs propres

StandardError=append:/opt/scalp/project/logs/mfe_mae.err.log

# sécurité
KillSignal=SIGINT
TimeoutStopSec=10

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

---- systemctl cat scalp-tunnel.service ----
# /etc/systemd/system/scalp-tunnel.service
[Unit]
Description=Scalp Cloudflare Named Tunnel
After=scalp-agent.service
Requires=scalp-agent.service

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
ExecStart=/usr/bin/cloudflared tunnel run scalp-agent
Restart=always
RestartSec=5
KillSignal=SIGTERM
TimeoutStopSec=10

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
